SQL> CREATE TABLE AIRLINE(

  3     AIRLINE_NAME VARCHAR(50),

  5          PRIMARY KEY (AIRLINE_ID),

  7  );

Table created.

 13  );

// 1. 1. List all airports in a Mumbai:


SQL> SELECT * FROM AIRPORT WHERE CITY = 'Mumbai';

AIRPORT_NAME                                       CITY                 STATE
-------------------------------------------------- -------------------- --------------------
Chhatrapati Shivaji Maharaj International Airport  Mumbai               Maharashtra




// 2.List all airlines operating in a Sardar Vallabhbhai Patel International Airport:


SQL> SELECT * FROM AIRLINE WHERE AIRPORT_NAME = 'Sardar Vallabhbhai Patel International Airport';

AIRLINE_ID AIRLINE_NAME                                       AIRPORT_NAME
---------- -------------------------------------------------- --------------------------------------------------
        22 Air India                                          Sardar Vallabhbhai Patel International Airport
        23 IndiGo                                             Sardar Vallabhbhai Patel International Airport
        24 SpiceJet                                           Sardar Vallabhbhai Patel International Airport




// 3. List all flights departing from a Mumbai (Chhatrapati Shivaji Maharaj International Airport):


SQL> SELECT * FROM FLIGHT WHERE SOURCE = 'Mumbai';

// 11.  SELECT PASSENGER NAME HAVING MULTIPLE PHONE NUMBERS:


SQL> SELECT P.NAME
  2  FROM PASSENGER P
  3  WHERE P.PASSPORT_NO IN
  4  (SELECT PPN.PASSPORT_NO
  5  FROM PASSENGER_PHONE_NO PPN
  6  GROUP BY PPN.PASSPORT_NO
  7  HAVING COUNT(*)>1);

// 13.find the average salary of employees in each city where the airport is located


SQL> SELECT A.CITY, AVG(E.SALARY) AS AVERAGE_SALARY 
     FROM  AIRPORT A 
     JOIN EMPLOYEE E 
     ON A.AIRPORT_NAME = E.AIRPORT_NAME 
     GROUP BY A.CITY;

CITY                 AVERAGE_SALARY
-------------------- --------------

Mumbai                        50100

// 14. SELECT NAME, PASSPORT NUMBER OF PASSENGERS WHERE CLASS IS Business :


SQL> SELECT P.NAME, P.PASSPORT_NO
  2  FROM PASSENGER P
  3  WHERE P.TICKET_NO IN
  4  (SELECT T.TICKET_NO
  5  FROM TICKET T
  6  WHERE T.CLASS = 'Business');

// 15.SELECT PASSENGER NAME, SEX, TICKET NUMBER HAVING FLIGHT DESTINATION AS New Delhi :


SQL> SELECT P.NAME, P.SEX, P.TICKET_NO
  2  FROM PASSENGER P
  3  WHERE P.FLIGHT_NO IN
  4  (SELECT F.FLIGHT_NO
  5  FROM FLIGHT F

// 1. Subquery to find all flights operated by Air India:


SQL> SELECT *
  2  FROM FLIGHT
  3  WHERE AIRLINE_ID IN
  4  (
  5     SELECT AIRLINE_ID
  6     FROM AIRLINE
  7     WHERE AIRLINE_NAME = 'Air India'
  8  );

// 2. Role-Based Access Control (RBAC):


SQL> CREATE ROLE C##Admin;

Role created.

SQL> GRANT SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE ON FLIGHT TO C##Admin;

Grant succeeded.

SQL>
